### [1] [Web-Native Graphical EMF Model Editors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11442)
*Susanne Göbel,Ralf Lämmel*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出EMFular，一个纯Web的EMF模型编辑框架，无需后端支持，基于Ecore模型生成可定制化图形编辑器，支持标准建模操作并与EMF保持一致，评估显示其在编辑能力、可定制性和生成鲁棒性方面表现良好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 图形化模型编辑正从桌面端向Web端迁移，现有框架存在不足，需要低工作量生成、高度可定制化以及易于部署的Web端模型编辑器。

Method: 通过分析现有框架特性，推导出一组设计原则，基于这些原则构建了纯Web框架EMFular。EMFular生成器将Ecore模型映射为基于Angular的图形编辑器，提供EMF一致性支持，并设有扩展点便于定制。

Result: EMFular生成的编辑器支持创建、检查、导航、编辑、撤销/重做等标准建模操作，并能处理包含关系和反向引用，与EMF保持一致性，支持与现有EMF工具的互操作。

Conclusion: EMFular在编辑器充分性、可适应性和生成鲁棒性方面通过了评估，证明其作为Web端EMF图形编辑框架的有效性。

Abstract: Graphical model editing is shifting from desktop applications to web-based tools. We analyze the characteristics of existing frameworks and, based on this analysis, we derive a set of design principles that imply low-effort generation, extensive customization possibilities, and straightforward deployment of the resulting editors. On these grounds, we introduce EMFular, a purely web-based framework for managing EMF models without any backend. The accompanying EMFular generator maps a given Ecore model (an EMF metamodel) to a ready-to-use and ready-to-customize graphical editor. EMFular editors provide 'EMF consistency', that is, they not only support standard modeling operations such as creation, inspection, navigation, editing, and undo/redo, but they also handle containment and inverse references in close alignment with EMF; they also provide interoperability with existing EMF tooling through compatible de-/serialization. A generated editor is an Angular project with designated extension points, which allows developers to customize and extend all aspects of the editor using the expressive power of Angular and its ecosystem, guided by the extension points of EMFular. We evaluate EMFular in terms of editor adequacy (available editing capabilities), adaptability (customization mechanisms and required effort), and robustness of the generation.

</details>


### [2] [Defeater Cards: Characterizing and Managing Safety Assurance Case Defeaters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11462)
*Usman Gohar,Michael C. Hunter,Salil Purandare,Jordan J. Rios,Myra B. Cohen,Robyn R. Lutz*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为“Defeater Cards”的结构化文档工具，用于系统性地识别、推理和管理安全案例中的反驳因素（defeaters）。该工具基于文献调查和5W1H框架设计，并通过跨领域案例研究验证了其有效性，同时开源了相关资源以促进社区应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 安全案例中的反驳因素（defeaters）对于质疑安全论证的有效性至关重要，但目前存在定义不一致、缺乏结构化支持、难以审查和缺乏文档标准等问题，亟需一种系统化的方法来管理这些反驳因素。

Method: 通过文献调查和主题分析，基于5W1H框架识别文档化标准，设计Defeater Cards的结构；通过两个跨领域案例研究验证其适用性，并开源相关卡片库以支持社区复用。

Result: Defeater Cards能够有效暴露隐藏假设、揭示推理缺口，并支持安全保证案例的持续演化；跨领域案例研究验证了其适用性和可复用性。

Conclusion: Defeater Cards为安全案例中的反驳因素提供了结构化、可追溯、可复用的文档化方法，有助于提升安全论证的严谨性和审查效率，开源资源将推动该方法的进一步应用和发展。

Abstract: Safety assurance cases provide structured justifications that safety-critical systems meet their safety requirements. Recently, the notion of defeaters has emerged as a rigorous means of challenging the validity of safety arguments. Examples of defeaters might include overly strict claims, unreliable evidence, or reasoning gaps. However, defeaters remain ad hoc, lack structured support for critical reflection, are inconsistently described, are difficult to review, and lack documentation standards. To address this, we propose Defeater Cards, a new structured documentation artifact for systematically characterizing, reasoning about, and managing defeaters in safety cases. Drawing on a literature survey and thematic analysis, we identify documentation criteria that inform the card's structure, based on the 5W1H framework. Defeater Cards are designed to support informed analysis and evolution, improve traceability and auditability, and enable the reuse of defeater knowledge across systems and product variants. We demonstrate their applicability through two cross-domain case studies, showing how they expose hidden assumptions, surface reasoning gaps, and support ongoing safety assurance case evolution. To support adoption and community reuse, we also release an open-source repository of defeater cards as a baseline upon which researchers and practitioners can build and describe lessons learned.

</details>


### [3] [SentTrack: Sentiment-Driven Bottleneck Detection in GitHub Issue Repositories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11476)
*Xinyu Hu,Ali Behbahani,Daniel Moon,Yaren Dogan,Nasir U. Eisty*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: SentTrack是一个双框架系统，通过分析GitHub issue讨论中的对话动态（而非代码指标），自动检测社会技术瓶颈。在AvaloniaUI仓库约9000个issue线程上验证，49%线程停滞，仅13%解决，系统可提前识别高风险讨论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有仓库健康工具过度聚焦代码指标，忽略了驱动或阻碍开发的对话动态。团队在issue线程中协调工作、报告bug、协商技术决策，但这些对话中的瓶颈缺乏自动化检测手段。

Method: 双管道框架：水平管道用LLM生成摘要，提取关注短语，经UMAP+HDBSCAN聚类（前3608个issue产出613个语义簇）；垂直管道用ABCDE协作框架分类每条评论，推断线程结果。加权评分引擎综合消极性、停滞、解决差距和线程长度。

Result: 全语料中49%线程停滞，仅13%解决，解决差距被识别为最主要的瓶颈信号。加权评分引擎可为维护者提供可解释的优先级排序工具。

Conclusion: SentTrack能有效从issue对话中自动检测工作流低效，情感信号可早于传统标签方法预警风险，并能从混合文本中分离人为叙述与机器噪声。

Abstract: Software engineering teams increasingly depend on GitHub issue threads to coordinate work, report bugs, and negotiate technical decisions, yet most repository health tools focus on code metrics and ignore the conversational dynamics that drive or stall development. This paper presents SentTrack, a dual-lens framework for detecting socio-technical bottlenecks from GitHub issue discussions. Applied to the AvaloniaUI open-source repository across approximately 9,000 issue threads, the framework addresses three questions: how to automate workflow-inefficiency detection from real-time conversational data, whether sentiment signals can surface risk earlier than traditional label-based methods, and how to isolate human narrative from machine-generated noise in mixed-media issue text. SentTrack combines two complementary pipelines. A horizontal pipeline translates raw issue reports into clean summaries using a large language model, extracts mid-level concern phrases, and clusters them through UMAP and HDBSCAN, producing 613 semantic clusters from the first 3,608 issues processed. A vertical pipeline applies the ABCDE collaborative interaction framework to classify each comment and infer thread-level outcomes. Across the full corpus, 49\% of threads ended in stagnation and only 13\% reached resolution, with the resolution gap identified as the dominant bottleneck signal. A weighted scoring engine that combines negativity, stagnation, resolution gap, and thread length gives maintainers an interpretable prioritization tool for high-friction discussions before they stall development.

</details>


### [4] [Acoda: Adversarial Code Obfuscation for Defending against LLM-based Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11755)
*Hongzhou Rao,Zikan Dong,Yanjie Zhao,Haodong Li,Haoyu Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于遗传算法的对抗性代码混淆框架Acoda，通过8种语义保持的混淆方法，有效防御LLM对源代码的分析，在7个先进LLM上实现高达70%的攻击成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在软件工程任务中广泛应用，但其强大的语义推理能力可能导致源代码逻辑被分析、重构甚至逆向工程，造成知识产权泄露风险。

Method: 提出Acoda框架，利用LLM的安全对齐和基于Token的信息处理两种机制，设计8种语义保持的混淆方法，通过遗传算法迭代优化混淆策略生成对抗样本，并构建基于LLM响应的定量评估框架。

Result: 在GPT-4o、DeepSeek、Qwen、Llama、Gemma等7个先进LLM上，Acoda实现了高达70%的攻击成功率，具有强跨模型迁移性和低运行时开销，且保持原始代码语义不变。

Conclusion: Acoda为LLM时代的代码保护和LLM安全防御提供了新视角，能有效诱导LLM拒绝或错误分析代码。

Abstract: With the widespread adoption of Large Language Models (LLMs) in software engineering (SE) tasks such as code understanding, debugging, and vulnerability detection, their powerful semantic reasoning ability has also introduced new security and privacy risks. LLMs can analyze, reconstruct, or even reverse-engineer source code logic, potentially leading to the leakage of intellectual property. To address this issue, we propose Acoda, a genetic algorithm-based adversarial code obfuscation framework that defends against LLM-based code analysis. Acoda leverages two key mechanisms of LLMs, namely safety alignment and token-based information processing, to design 8 semantics-preserving obfuscation methods. It iteratively optimizes obfuscation strategies through a genetic algorithm to generate adversarial samples that maximize defensive effectiveness. In addition, we propose a quantitative evaluation framework based on LLM responses, which combines an auxiliary LLM and four evaluation metrics to assess how target LLMs analyze obfuscated code comprehensively. Experimental results show that Acoda can effectively induce LLMs to refuse or misinterpret code analysis. On 7 state-of-the-art LLMs, including GPT-4o, DeepSeek, Qwen, Llama, and Gemma, Acoda achieves an attack success rate (ASR) of up to 70%, with strong cross-model transferability and minimal runtime overhead, while ensuring that the semantics of the original code remain unchanged. Overall, this study provides a new perspective for code protection and LLM security defense in the era of LLMs.

</details>


### [5] [Understanding and Detecting Scalability Faults in Large-Scale Distributed Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11815)
*Hao-Nan Zhu,Goodness Ayinmode,Cesar A. Stuardo,Haryadi S. Gunawi,Cindy Rubio-González*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过分析444个可扩展性故障报告，发现大多数故障由维度代码片段与反模式协同导致，并提出了结合动态和静态分析的ScaleLens方法来检测这些故障，相比基线方法检测效果提升4.2倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着分布式系统规模增长，系统复杂性导致可扩展性故障频发，这些故障具有潜伏性且难以诊断，现有研究对此缺乏系统性理解与有效检测手段。

Method: 首先对10个大规模分布式系统的444个可扩展性问题报告进行系统研究，归纳常见反模式与根因；然后基于发现设计ScaleLens方法，结合动态分析与静态分析来定位维度代码片段并匹配相应反模式。

Result: ScaleLens检测维度代码片段的数量是基线方法的4.2倍；在Cassandra、HDFS和Ignite的最新稳定版本中检测出334个存在确认问题的维度代码片段。

Conclusion: ScaleLens能够有效检测可扩展性故障，显著优于现有基线方法，为大规模分布式系统的可扩展性问题诊断提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Scalable distributed systems form the backbone of modern computing infrastructure. However, as scale grows, system complexity may lead to scalability faults. Scalability faults are challenging to uncover and diagnose, as they are often latent and only manifest at large-scale deployment. In this paper, we present the first comprehensive study on scalability faults and propose an approach for their detection. First, we systematically investigate 444 scalability issue reports from 10 large-scale distributed systems to understand the common anti-patterns and root causes of scalability faults. We found that the majority of these faults are caused by the synergy between dimensional code fragments and anti-patterns associated with them. Second, based on our findings, we design and implement ScaleLens, a novel approach to detect scalability faults. ScaleLens combines dynamic and static analyses to pinpoint dimensional code fragments and match them with anti-patterns. Our evaluation shows that ScaleLens detects 4.2x more dimensional code fragments associated with known scalability faults compared to the baseline. On the latest stable versions of Cassandra, HDFS, and Ignite, ScaleLens detects 334 dimensional code fragments with confirmed problematic behavior.

</details>


### [6] [How Requirements Quality Makes (or Breaks) Traceability Link Recovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11834)
*Tobias Hey,Julian Frattini*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文研究了需求质量缺陷对需求与源码之间自动追踪链接恢复（TLR）性能的影响，发现某些缺陷会降低TLR性能，而另一些反而有益，且不同TLR方法对缺陷的响应不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 需求中的质量缺陷会影响后续的追踪链接恢复活动，但目前缺乏相关的实证证据，作者旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 在189个用例描述中标注了28种质量缺陷，应用五种不同的TLR方法，通过统计检验量化缺陷对TLR性能的影响强度。

Result: 某些质量缺陷（如不以名词短语开头的句子）会损害TLR性能，而另一些（如包含实现细节的用例）反而有益；不同类型的TLR方法对缺陷的响应不同。

Conclusion: 选择最优TLR方法需根据数据集的质量特征而定，不同质量缺陷对TLR性能的影响具有差异性。

Abstract: Traceability information between requirements and source code greatly benefits the maintenance of a software system. Since manually establishing trace links is cumbersome and error-prone, previous research explored automated traceability link recovery (TLR) approaches to support this task. However, quality defects in requirements impact subsequent activities such as TLR, yet evidence about this remains scarce. Our objective is to contribute empirical evidence on this impact. At the same time, we aim to understand how the performance of TLR approaches varies given these quality defects. To this end, we annotated 28 types of quality defect in 189 use case descriptions from two datasets. Then, we executed five distinct TLR approaches on the dataset and measured their performance in recovering trace links. Finally, we performed statistical tests to quantify the defects' effect strength on this performance. Our results show that some quality defects harm TLR performance, e.g., sentences that do not start with noun phrases, while others actually benefit performance, e.g., use cases that include implementation details. Moreover, different types of approaches respond differently to these defects. As a consequence, the performance-optimizing choice of a TLR approach depends on the quality of the dataset.

</details>


### [7] [Enhancing LLM-Based Code Translation with Verified Multi-Semantic Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11863)
*Yufu Wang,He Jiang,Hao Lin,Peiyu Zou,Ang Jia,Xiaochen Li,Zhilei Ren*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出Multisage框架，通过多语义增强与自校准机制提升LLM代码翻译的可靠性，在HumanEval-X基准上将翻译成功率提升最高2.22倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM代码翻译方法依赖词级统计模式而非程序语义理解，导致翻译结果存在逻辑和语义错误。虽然功能描述和测试用例等高质量语义指导可缓解此问题，但实际场景中这些资源往往不可用。因此，核心挑战是如何从源代码中直接构建丰富的语义信息，并确保其准确可靠地指导翻译。

Method: Multisage框架包含三个模块：1) 语义表示解析模块：从源代码提取数据流图、类型约束和外部API信息等结构化基础语义；2) 多语义增强模块：基于基础语义生成代码摘要、函数级测试用例、API描述与测试等多种增强语义；3) 语义一致性校准模块：通过语义保持变异和跨语义一致性验证，对生成语义进行过滤、校准和精炼。

Result: 在HumanEval-X基准上，Multisage将翻译成功率最高提升2.22倍，持续优于普通提示、指令微调LLM和思维链推理方法，其中小型模型提升最为显著。

Conclusion: 显式的语义增强能够显著提升LLM代码翻译的可靠性，验证了结构化语义信息在代码翻译任务中的关键价值。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have shown great promise for automated code translation, yet existing approaches often rely on token-level statistical patterns rather than sufficient understanding of program semantics. As a result, translated programs may still contain logical and semantic errors. Although high-quality semantic guidance, such as functional descriptions and test cases, can help mitigate these errors, such resources are often unavailable in real-world scenarios. This raises two key challenges: how to construct rich semantic information directly from source code, and how to ensure that such semantics are accurate and reliable enough to guide translation.To address these challenges, we propose Multisage, a multi-semantic augmentation and self-calibration framework for LLM-based code translation. Multisage consists of three modules. First, a semantic representation parsing module extracts structured base semantics from source code, including data-flow graphs, type constraints, and external API information. Second, a multi-semantic augmentation module builds on these representations to generate diverse augmented semantics, including code summaries, function-level test cases, and API-oriented descriptions and tests. Third, a semantic consistency calibration module uses semantics-preserving mutations and cross-semantic consistency verification to filter, calibrate, and refine the generated semantics.Experiments on the HumanEval-X code translation benchmark show that Multisage improves translation success rates by up to 2.22 times across diverse backbone models. It consistently outperforms vanilla prompting, instruction-tuned LLMs, and Chain-of-Thought reasoning, with the largest gains observed on smaller models. These results demonstrate that explicit semantic augmentation can substantially improve the reliability of LLM-based code translation.

</details>


### [8] [Agents All the Way Down; A Methodology for Building Custom AI Agents from Substrate to Production](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11869)
*Marc Alier Forment,Juanan Pereira,Francisco José García-Peñalvo,María José Casañ Guerrero*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出"Agents All the Way Down"方法论，系统化描述如何端到端构建定制AI Agent，包含两个前提条件（P1：将LLM作为软件组件；P2：构建模块）和三个实践循环（P3:用通用Agent原型；P4:将结果打包为CLI；P5:用Agent测试Agent），并基于AAC项目实践验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前缺乏系统化的方法论来指导如何端到端构建定制AI Agent，相关实践散落在播客、博客和泄露的系统提示中，没有统一的书面规范。

Method: 提出"Agents All the Way Down"方法论：两个前提条件（P1 Substrate、P2 Building blocks）加上三个实践（P3原型、P4打包为CLI的Turtle模式、P5 Agent测试Agent），形成P3→P4→P5的迭代循环。

Result: 基于AAC（LAMB平台上的定制Agent）项目验证，由一位开发者在约10天内借助AI结对编程完成并投入生产。该方法论与语言和框架无关。

Conclusion: 该论文系统性记录了定制AI Agent的构建实践，提出"Agents All the Way Down"方法论，并指出多Agent编排本质上是CLI组合。

Abstract: Custom AI agents areagents that live inside their own
  application, talk to their own data and tools, enforce their own security boundaries,
  and carry their own brand and audit trail. What separates them from the general-purpose
  tier is fit, not capability: each is built for one job, by the
  engineer who will maintain it. No published practice sets out how to build one end to
  end. The pieces are everywhere (function-calling APIs, the Model Context Protocol, code
  agents to pair with), but the practice that chains them lives in podcasts, blogs, and
  leaked system prompts. This paper writes that practice down as a methodology, Agents All
  the Way Down: two preconditions crossed once and kept, then three practices repeated
  for the agent's life. The preconditions are (P1) Substrate, the LLM as a software
  component, framed as tools, then system, then messages under prompt-caching; and (P2)
  Building blocks: function calling, MCP, CLI orchestration, the liteshell pattern, the
  agent loop, skills, characters, hooks, and scaffolding. The practices are (P3) prototype
  with a general-purpose agent; (P4) harvest, fold, and ship the result as a CLI, the
  Turtle pattern; and (P5) agent-tests-agent, in which a general-purpose agent drives it
  through behavioural scenarios, a complement to classical testing, not a replacement. The
  working loop is P3 to P4 to P5 and back, and one corollary falls out for free:
  multi-agent orchestration is just CLI composition. The methodology is framework-free by
  construction. It was distilled from the AAC, a custom agent for the open-source LAMB
  platform, built in about ten days by one developer with an AI pair-programmer and in
  production . We present it as a transferable practice, independent of any language or framework.

</details>


### [9] [Characterizing Software Aging in GPU-Based LLM Serving Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11916)
*Domenico Cotroneo,Bojan Cukic*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对基于GPU的大型语言模型（LLM）服务系统的软件老化实证研究方法。通过在六个同地部署上运行216小时的压力测试，结合统计分析，发现所有部署均存在显著的内存老化现象，且泄漏率与运行时和配置高度相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统软件老化研究主要针对CPU密集型系统和规律性负载，而LLM服务系统具有Python主机+CUDA设备、请求成本差异大、软件栈快速演进等特点，现有方法不适用，亟需新的研究框架。

Method: 在六个同地部署上开展216小时压力测试，并行监控主机、设备和客户端指标，采用考虑自相关性和多重检验的统计流水线进行分析。

Result: 所有部署均表现出统计上显著的内存老化，泄漏率强烈依赖于服务运行时和部署配置。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一个可复现的框架，开辟了软件老化与再生研究与LLM服务系统交叉领域的新方向。

Abstract: This paper proposes an empirical methodology to study software aging in GPU-based LLM serving systems. Traditional aging studies focus on CPU-centric software with relatively regular workloads; LLM serving is different, spanning a Python host and a CUDA device, handling requests whose cost varies by orders of magnitude, and relying on rapidly evolving software stacks. We run a 216-hour campaign across six co-located deployments under identical stress conditions, monitor host, device, and client metrics in parallel, and apply a statistical pipeline that accounts for autocorrelation and multiple testing. Our results reveal statistically significant memory aging in all deployments, with leak rates strongly dependent on the serving runtime and deployment configuration. Beyond these findings, we provide a reproducible framework that opens a research direction at the intersection of the software aging and rejuvenation and LLM serving communities.

</details>


### [10] [Exploration Structure in LLM Agents for Multi-File Change Localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11976)
*Akeela Darryl Fattha,Kia Ying Chua,Lingxiao Jiang,Laura Wynter*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文研究软件工程中基于LLM的文件定位方法，提出非线性、领域并行的多智能体探索优于传统线性探索，尤其在跨子系统变更场景下表现更好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI智能体线性探索代码库的方式与跨子系统变更的结构性不匹配，需要更高效的探索策略。

Method: 构建持久会话评估方法，设计领域作用域并行智能体文件遍历系统，与多种基线（纯LLM、单智能体RLM、外部CLI）在SWE Bench Pro基准上对比。

Result: 小型Haiku类模型的领域并行智能体在同类模型中微F1最高；领域智能体仅次Codex 5.5 High；原始基准上大模型Sonnet精度高但召回率低。

Abstract: Software engineering tools increasingly rely on LLM based agents to localize files to change to resolve a software issue. Most AI agents explore repositories linearly, that is, visiting one directory or file per step. We postulate that this is a structural mismatch for changes that span several subsystems. We compare linear sequential exploration against non-linear, domain-scoped parallel agentic exploration. Using SWE Bench Pro as initial benchmark, we focus on ansible as an exemplar. We construct an approach for persistent-session evaluation of GitHub issues anchored at a single base commit. We compare our non-linear domain-agent file traversal system against a base LLM without direct repository access, a single agent Recursive Language Model (RLM) baseline with a persistent Python REPL and an external CLI baseline using Codex 5.5 High. Domain scoped parallel agent spawning with a small Haiku-class model achieves the highest micro F1 among Haiku class models by a large margin. Domain-agents is the second highest behind only the much larger Codex 5.5 High on our own expanded benchmark including over more recent PRs from 2025 and 2026. On the original, curated, 2020 SWE-bench Pro benchmark, a larger Sonnet plain LLM baseline attains higher micro F1 by predicting few files, leading to higher precision, but at significantly lower all gold recall. We also present three additional findings. First, documentation evolution is a latent dependency unresolved by any approach. Second, naive file system access can degrade localization driven by test-file over prediction. Lastly, forced multi-agent consultation does not measurably help and raises token cost substantially.

### [11] [Undefined Behavior in C and C++: An Experiment With Desktop Use Cases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12064)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: C/C++中的未定义行为虽被广泛认知，但其在实际日常桌面使用中的普遍程度缺乏系统性的实证研究。

Method: 在Linux发行版中，使用编译器实现的未定义行为消毒器（sanitizer）进行检测，通过完成59个简单实验任务，收集并分析产生的未定义行为警告。

Result: 59个任务产生了近11000条独特警告，涉及32个独特程序/库；多数来自Mesa图形库；登录GNOME产生超500条警告；绝大多数警告与虚表指针有关；栈追踪普遍较长。

Conclusion: C/C++程序中的未定义行为在日常桌面使用中非常普遍，该研究为C/C++的实证文献做出了贡献。

Abstract: Undefined behavior is idiomatic to C and C++ programming; such behavior is a use of an erroneous program construct for which the languages impose no requirements, such as integer overflows. The paper presents an empirical experiment seeking to probe the extent of undefined behavior executing underneath typical desktop use of a Linux distribution. The analysis is based on an undefined behavior sanitizer implemented in a compiler. According to the results, undefined behavior is common. By completing 59 simple experimental tasks, nearly 11 thousand unique undefined behavior warnings were generated by 32 unique programs and libraries written in C or C++. Of these warnings, most were associated with the Mesa graphics library and generated by interacting with graphical user interfaces. Merely logging into the GNOME desktop environment generated over 500 unique warnings. Of all warnings, the clear majority was about virtual table pointers. The associated stack traces were also lengthy in general. With these and other results, the paper contributes to the empirical literature on C and C++.

### [12] [Mind your key: An Empirical Study of LLM API Credential Leakage in iOS Apps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12212)
*Pinran Gao,Lingxiang Wang,Ying Zhang,Fan Yang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文首次系统研究了iOS应用中LLM API密钥泄漏问题。通过对444个应用的动态分析，发现282个应用（63.5%）存在可被利用的凭证泄漏，包括JWT令牌泄漏、未认证后端代理和明文API密钥三种模式。三个月后的重新评估显示，仅28%的漏洞被修复，表明问题普遍且持久。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型（LLM）集成到移动应用中带来了新的凭证安全风险——泄漏的凭证可被用于未经授权调用LLM推理服务，给开发者造成经济损失。此前凭证泄漏研究主要聚焦Android应用，尚无研究系统调查iOS应用中LLM API密钥泄漏问题。

Method: 构建包含444个iOS应用的高质量数据集（从1092个候选中筛选），开发了LLMKeyLens动态分析框架，通过流量拦截、提供商特定密钥提取和主动有效性确认来检测LLM API密钥泄漏，无需源代码访问或二进制解密。

Result: 282个应用暴露了可被利用的LLM API凭证，覆盖至少10个提供商。识别出三种泄漏模式：JWT令牌泄漏（48%）、未认证后端代理访问（33%）、明文API密钥传输（19%）。三个月后重新评估，仅28%修复了漏洞，72%仍可被利用。

Conclusion: LLM API密钥泄漏在iOS生态系统中普遍且持久，暴露出开发者实践与安全集成原则之间的系统性差距。安全的LLM集成不仅需要开发者意识提升，还需要提供商提供明确的安全指导以及平台层面的强制执行机制。

Abstract: The rapid integration of large language models (LLMs) into mobile applications has introduced a new class of credential security risk: leaked credentials that grant unauthorized access to LLM inference services, causing financial damage to developers. Prior work on credential leakage has focused primarily on Android apps; to date, no empirical study has systematically investigated LLM API key leakage in iOS applications.
  We present the first in-depth empirical study of API key leakage in LLM-integrated apps. We construct a high-quality dataset of 444 iOS applications, filtered from 1092 candidates through a standardized process, and develop LLMKeyLens, a dynamic analysis framework that detects LLM API key leakage via traffic interception, provider-specific key extraction, and active validity confirmation, requiring neither source code access nor binary decryption. Our analysis reveals that 282 applications expose exploitable LLM API credentials in network traffic, spanning at least ten providers. We identify three leakage patterns: JWT-based token leakage (48%), unauthenticated backend proxy access (33%), and plaintext API key transmission (19%). To assess remediation, we re-analyzed the same 282 vulnerable applications three months after responsible disclosure; only 28% had remediated the reported vulnerability, while 72% remained exploitable, with persistent issues stemming from unauthenticated backends and broken JWT implementations.
  Our findings show that LLM API key leakage is both prevalent and persistent in the iOS ecosystem, exposing a systemic gap between developer practice and secure integration principles, and suggest that secure LLM integration requires not only developer awareness but also explicit security guidance from providers and platform-level enforcement.

</details>


### [13] [Rule Taxonomy and Evolution in AI IDEs: A Mining and Survey Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12231)
*Guangzong Cai,Ruiyin Li,Peng Liang,Zengyang Li,Mojtaba Shahin*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过混合方法实证研究了AI IDE中的"规则"工件，建立了包含5个主类别和25个子类别的分类体系，发现开发者认为重要的架构约束在实际配置中较少，规则更新能显著提升工件合规率（平均提升22.99%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI IDE中"规则"作为新型软件工件，允许开发者向LLM注入项目特定约束，但其分类体系、演化规律和实际影响尚未被系统探索。

Method: 混合方法实证研究：挖掘83个开源项目提取7,310条规则建立分类体系，结合99位从业者的问卷调查进行三角验证，并对1,540个规则演化事件和160个工件合规性评估进行分析。

Result: 建立了5主类25子类的规则分类体系；开发者重视架构约束但实际仓库中多为低层级工作流和代码格式约束；规则更新频繁，驱动因素主要是上下文扩展（29.17%）和丰富（26.59%）；开发者修改规则主要为了纠正AI错误（77.78%）；规则更新使工件平均合规率从49.14%提升至72.13%。

Conclusion: 研究为开发者优化提示策略和工具构建者设计AI IDE的自动冲突检测与上下文管理机制提供了实证依据。

Abstract: The adoption of AI-powered Integrated Development Environments (AI IDEs) has introduced "Rules" as a novel software artifact, allowing developers to persistently inject project-specific constraints and architectural guidelines into the context of Large Language Models (LLMs). Despite their role in aligning AI behavior with developer intent, the taxonomy, evolution, and practical impact of these rules remain largely unexplored. To bridge this gap, we conducted a mixed-methods empirical study on AI IDE rules. By mining 83 open-source projects and extracting 7,310 rules, we established a comprehensive taxonomy comprising 5 primary and 25 secondary categories. We then triangulated these artifacts with survey responses from 99 practitioners. Our analysis identified a contrast between developer priorities and actual configurations: while practitioners rate architectural constraints as highly important, rule files in repositories primarily consist of low-level workflow and code formatting constraints. Furthermore, our analysis of 1,540 rule evolution events revealed that rules are updated frequently. Repository data further indicate that rule evolution is primarily driven by constructive context expansions (29.17%) and enrichments (26.59%). In contrast, surveyed developers reported modifying rules primarily to correct AI errors (77.78%), typically by adding new negative constraints rather than editing existing ones. Finally, an artifact compliance assessment of 160 rule evolution events revealed that updating rules significantly improves the adherence of software artifacts, with the average artifact compliance rate increasing by 22.99% (from 49.14% to 72.13%) following an update. Our study provides empirical insights that can help developers optimize prompting strategies and guide tool builders in designing automated conflict-detection and context-management mechanisms for AI IDEs.

</details>

### [14] [TileFuse: A Fused Mixed-Precision Kernel Library for Efficient Quantized LLM Inference on AMD NPUs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11357)
*Wesley Pang,Gregory Hyegang Jun,Feiyang Liu,Deming Chen*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: TileFuse是一个针对AMD XDNA2 NPU的混合精度内核库，通过融合解包、反量化和矩阵计算，实现了AWQ风格的W4A16/W8A16量化格式，在边缘LLM推理中显著提升性能和能效（GEMM提升121.6%，GEMV提升281%，端到端预填充延迟降低2倍，能耗降低64.6%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 边缘SoC集成的NPU在部署LLM时面临挑战：广泛使用的量化格式（如AWQ）与现有NPU软件栈不兼容，后者通常是专有的且底层控制有限，导致模型需被迫适配NPU特定的量化方案。

Method: TileFuse采用协同设计方法，融合权重布局、元数据放置、混合精度微内核和阵列级数据流。具体包括：将解包、反量化与GEMM/GEMV执行融合为单一内核流程；引入交错预分块布局以支持高达32K的GEMM维度；重新设计GEMV数据流以充分利用4x8 AIE阵列。

Result: 内核层面：GEMM性能提升121.6%，GEMV性能提升281%，相比iGPU基线在GEMM上实现2倍以上的性能和能效提升。端到端LLM实验：预填充延迟降低2倍，能耗降低64.6%以上。

Conclusion: XDNA2是AWQ风格边缘LLM推理的实用目标，NPU原生支持现成量化方案可大幅提升NPU在客户端部署中的可用性。

Abstract: With the growing demand for on-device LLM inference, edge SoCs increasingly integrate NPUs to improve performance and energy efficiency under tight power and thermal budgets. However, practical LLM deployment on current client NPUs remains difficult: widely used quantization formats such as AWQ do not map cleanly onto many existing NPU software stacks, which are often proprietary and expose limited low-level control. In this work, we present \textit{TileFuse}, a close-to-metal mixed-precision kernel library for AMD XDNA2 NPUs that targets transformer linear layers in quantized LLM inference. TileFuse brings practical low-bit formats such as AWQ-style W4A16 and W8A16 directly onto XDNA2, rather than forcing the model to be reshaped around an NPU-specific quantization scheme.
  TileFuse co-designs weight layout, metadata placement, mixed-precision microkernels, and array-level dataflow. Specifically, it fuses unpacking, dequantization, and GEMM/GEMV execution into a single kernel flow, introduces an interleaved pre-tiling layout that supports GEMM dimensions up to 32K, and redesigns GEMV dataflow to utilize the full 4x8 AIE array. Across kernel-level evaluations, TileFuse improves performance by up to 121.6% for GEMM and 281% for GEMV over full-precision baselines, while delivering more than 2x performance and energy-efficiency gains over strong iGPU baselines on GEMM. In end-to-end LLM experiments on Ryzen AI laptops, TileFuse achieves up to 2.0x lower prefilling latency with more than 64.6% lower energy consumption. Together, these results show that XDNA2 is a practical target for AWQ-style edge LLM inference and that native NPU support for off-the-shelf quantization can make NPUs substantially more usable in real client deployments.

</details>


### [15] [Beyond Per-Token Pricing: A Concurrency-Aware Methodology for LLM Infrastructure Cost Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11690)
*Chitral Patil*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 现有LLM成本计算器错误地将GPU利用率视为固定输入，导致成本估算偏差高达36.3倍。本文提出基于实际流量的测量方法，开源vllm-cost-meter工具，并通过实验验证了负载、模型架构和硬件对实际成本的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有开源成本计算器都将GPU利用率作为用户输入的固定参数（或默认100%），从未与实际负载挂钩，导致自托管成本被系统性低估，尤其对低流量场景误导严重。

Method: 提出C_eff = f(H, M, Q, λ, L)的参数化测量方法，在H100和A100上对Dense、Ultra-sparse MoE、Sparse MoE三类模型进行42+56次基准测试，开发vllm-cost-meter工具实时接入vLLM服务器报告实际每百万token成本。

Result: 相同H100硬件上每百万token成本跨度$0.21-$15.25，低负载下成本偏差2.5-24x（1-10 rps），接近空闲时达36.3x。FP8量化对MoE架构吞吐提升69-74%，是Dense模型（+31%）的2.2-2.4倍。A100上负载偏差7.0-11.4x，且FP8优势在缺乏原生FP8张量核心的硬件上消失。

Conclusion: 负载是自托管成本估算中最大的误差源，成本计算器必须将实际流量纳入考量；有效参数数量（而非总模型大小）是饱和经济性的主要预测因子；硬件条件对量化策略的有效性有决定性影响。

Abstract: Every public LLM cost calculator we surveyed treats GPU utilization as a fixed input -- entered by the user, baked in as a preset, or silently assumed at 100% -- never measured against the operator's actual load. We show that this assumption is the dominant source of error: on identical H100 hardware, effective cost spans \$0.21 to \$15.25 per million output tokens, an underutilization penalty of 2.5-24x across low-to-moderate enterprise loads (1-10 rps) and up to 36.3x near idle -- driven by one operator-controlled variable, offered request rate lambda, which sets in-flight concurrency via Little's Law and which no open-source calculator exposes. Because calculators take utilization as a user-supplied input, any utilization-naive estimate understates true cost by exactly 1/U, systematically mispricing self-hosting -- most severely over-selling it for low-traffic workloads. We propose a measurement methodology that parameterizes the relationship as C_eff = f(H, M, Q, lambda, L), validate it with 42 benchmarks across dense, ultra-sparse MoE, and sparse MoE models, and release vllm-cost-meter, an open-source cost meter that attaches to a live vLLM server and reports real \$/M-tokens against the operator's own traffic. We further show that FP8 quantization benefits the MoE architectures we tested roughly 2.2-2.4x more than the dense model (+69 to +74% vs. +31% peak throughput; n=3, broader validation needed), and our data are consistent with active parameter count, not total model size, being a primary predictor of saturation economics. To rule out single-hardware confounding we repeat the core sweep on A100 80GB PCIe (56 runs): the load-driven spread reproduces at 7.0-11.4x, the active-parameters ordering survives at FP8, and the dense-FP8 advantage inverts on silicon without native FP8 tensor cores -- a hardware-conditional caveat the framework already accommodates.

</details>

*Niccolò D Archivio*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文研究了3-Majority和2-Choices两种共识动态在完全图上的收敛时间，发现其由初始意见最大密度这一局部参数决定，而非全局参数如意见数量或ℓ2范数，并给出了对任意初始配置在log因子内匹配的紧界。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过理论分析建立3-Majority和2-Choices动态的收敛时间与初始意见最大密度___α(0)___∞之间的精确关系，给出Θ(·)的上下界。

Result: 3-Majority在Θ(min{___α(0)___∞^{-1}, √n})轮内以高概率达成共识；2-Choices在Θ(___α(0)___∞^{-1})轮内以高概率达成共识。

Abstract: We establish the correct parameter governing the convergence time of the 3-Majority and 2-Choices dynamics on the complete graph in the synchronous model. Recent work [Shimizu and Shiraga, PODC'25] provides matching upper and lower bounds on the number of rounds to consensus, but only in a weak sense: the bounds are shown to coincide for some initial opinion configuration.  In contrast, we obtain tight bounds in a strong sense, with upper and lower bounds matching up to logarithmic factors for every initial configuration. Let $α$ (0) be the initial opinion-frequency vector, and denote by ___$α$ (0) ___ $\infty$ its maximum entry. We show that 3-Majority reaches consensus in $Θ$(min{___$α$ (0) ___ -1 $\infty$ , $\sqrt$ n}) rounds w.h.p., while 2-Choices reaches consensus in $Θ$(___$α$ (0) ___ -1 $\infty$ ) rounds w.h.p. Our results demonstrate that the convergence time of both dynamics is governed not by global parameters such as the number of opinions k or the squared ${\ell}$ 2 norm of the initial opinion distribution, but rather by the ''local'' parameter ___$α$ (0) ___ $\infty$ , the maximum initial opinion density.

### [18] [Harnessing Routing Foresight for Micro-step-level MoE load balancing in RL Post-training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11867)
*Yuming Zhou,Haoyang Li,Sheng Lin,Yanfeng Zhao,Tong Zhao,Xupeng Miao,Jie Jiang,Fangcheng Fu,Bin Cui*

TL;DR: ForeMoE是一个面向MoE强化学习后训练的微步级负载均衡系统，利用多阶段RL流水线中的可预见路由信息，通过分层规划器和传输引擎实现高效负载均衡，在64GPU上达到最高1.45倍加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有负载均衡系统针对预训练设计，依赖历史步级统计量，但在RL后训练中微步级批处理量极小导致高频负载波动，无法有效应对。

Method: 利用RL多阶段流水线（rollout、recompute、policy update）中rollout阶段的可预见路由信息主动引导后续阶段负载均衡；采用分层规划器将NP-hard问题分解为可解子问题；设计传输引擎利用CPU辅助和GPU直连互补路径实现专家重叠传输。

Result: 在64GPU上，相比于最先进的RL后训练系统，ForeMoE实现了最高1.45倍的加速比。

Conclusion: ForeMoE通过微步级负载均衡有效解决了MoE模型在RL后训练中的负载不均衡问题，显著提升了训练效率。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) and reinforcement learning (RL) post-training now dominate large language model (LLM) development, yet expert load imbalance remains a critical challenge. Existing load-balancing systems target pre-training by relying on historical step-level statistics. However, these methods fail under the unique workload dynamics of RL post-training: the step-level load is stable, but the tiny batch sizes processed during micro-steps cause severe, high-frequency load fluctuations.
  We introduce ForeMoE, a micro-step-level load balancing system for MoE RL post-training. Instead of relying on historical statistics, ForeMoE exploits the multi-stage RL pipeline (rollout, recompute, policy update) by using foreseeable routing information from the rollout stage to proactively guide load balancing in the remaining stages. To support frequent per-micro-step reconfiguration, ForeMoE employs a hierarchical planner that decomposes the NP-hard load balancing problem into tractable sub-components, alongside a transfer engine that leverages complementary hardware paths (CPU-assisted and GPU-direct) for overlapped expert transfer. Evaluations on 64 GPUs demonstrate that ForeMoE achieves up to a 1.45$\times$ speedup over state-of-the-art RL post-training systems.

</details>


### [19] [From Fork-Join to Asynchronous Tasks: Parallelizing Tiled Cholesky Decomposition with OpenMP and HPX](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11937)
*Alexander Strack,Alexander Van Craen,Dirk Pflüger*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文通过Cholesky分解基准测试，在128核AMD系统上比较了OpenMP与HPX异步多任务运行时在四种并行变体下的性能，发现HPX在最优分块大小下比OpenMP快15%-30%，异步任务快26%，任务开销小3.8倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管OpenMP的fork-join并行模型广泛使用，但其隐式同步屏障对负载不均的算法有性能惩罚；异步多任务运行时虽能规避此问题，但实际性能优势缺乏量化评估。

Method: 设计了Cholesky-Bench基准，在双插槽128核AMD Zen 2节点上，对右视Cholesky分解的四种并行变体（经典fork-join、折叠fork-join、同步任务、异步依赖任务）分别使用GCC/LLVM的OpenMP和HPX运行时进行测试。

Result: HPX在所有变体中优于OpenMP，最优分块下快15%-30%；异步HPX任务比OpenMP快26%，任务开销低3.8倍；折叠fork-join缩小了与同步任务的差距；消除冗余同步屏障带来7%（OpenMP）至14%（HPX）的提升。

Conclusion: 异步多任务运行时HPX在非均匀负载场景下性能显著优于OpenMP，且编译器实现差异对fork-join调度和任务创建开销有显著影响。

Abstract: Fork-join parallelism, popularized by OpenMP, remains the dominant model for shared-memory parallel programming, but its implicit synchronization barriers can penalize algorithms with inhomogeneous workloads. Asynchronous many-task (AMT) runtimes sidestep these barriers by expressing work as a dependency graph of fine-grained tasks. Yet, the actual performance benefit over a carefully written fork-join baseline is rarely quantified. In this work, we introduce Cholesky-Bench and use it to revisit the tiled Cholesky decomposition, a canonical irregular kernel, comparing four parallelization variants of the right-looking algorithm across two runtimes: the OpenMP implementations shipped with GCC and LLVM, and the HPX AMT runtime. The variants span classical fork-join, a collapsed fork-join that exposes additional inner-loop parallelism, synchronous tasking, and asynchronous tasking with explicit data dependencies. We benchmark all eight combinations on a dual-socket 128-core AMD Zen 2 node across multiple tile sizes and problem sizes. Our results show that across all variants, HPX outperforms OpenMP at the optimal tile size by 15%-30%. Specifically, asynchronous HPX tasks are up to 26% faster than their OpenMP counterparts, and exhibit roughly 3.8x smaller task overhead. Furthermore, the collapsed fork-join variants close most of the gap to synchronous tasking. Removing redundant synchronization barriers yields an additional improvement of 7% (OpenMP) to 14% (HPX). A GCC-versus-LLVM comparison further reveals compiler-specific differences in fork-join scheduling and task-creation overheads.

### [21] [Efficient and Robust Online Learning to Rank in Decentralized Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12246)
*Marcel Gregoriadis,Martijn de Vos,Sayan Biswas,Anne-Marie Kermarrec,Johan Pouwelse*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 提出RankGuard，一种去中心化的在线学习排序框架，通过基于用户私有点击历史验证模型更新来防御投毒攻击，首次提供了形式化收敛保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有在线学习排序系统依赖可信中心服务器，存在运营商引入偏见的问题；去中心化学习虽可避免中心化风险，但面临恶意节点投毒攻击的威胁。

Method: RankGuard让用户直接交换模型更新，通过将传入模型与用户私有点击历史（已纠正位置偏差）对比，仅当模型能比当前本地模型更好地解释用户过往交互时才进行聚合，从而防御投毒攻击。

Result: 在四个标准基准和三种点击模型下，针对四种投毒攻击（含自适应攻击），RankGuard在多数场景下优于所有基线方法，且效率比最接近的竞品高62倍。

Conclusion: RankGuard是首个具备形式化收敛保证的去中心化OLTR算法，能有效防御投毒攻击，同时保持高效性。

Abstract: In Online Learning to Rank (OLTR), ranking models are trained directly from live user interactions, but existing systems rely on a trusted central server to collect and process these interactions. This leaves operators free to introduce biases that conflict with user interests. Decentralized learning offers an attractive alternative, allowing users to collaboratively train a shared ranking model by exchanging model updates directly with one another, without any central authority. In such settings, however, malicious nodes can send poisoned model updates that degrade the ranking quality of honest nodes. We introduce RankGuard, a decentralized OLTR framework in which users collaboratively train ranking models and exchange model updates directly with other nodes. RankGuard defends against poisoning attacks by carefully evaluating incoming models against the user's own private click history, corrected for position bias. An incoming model is only aggregated if it better explains the user's past interactions than the current local model, making it fundamentally hard for malicious nodes to craft updates that pass this test without also genuinely helping the user. We derive a theoretical convergence guarantee of RankGuard. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first formal convergence analysis of a decentralized OLTR algorithm. We evaluate RankGuard against four poisoning attacks, including a powerful adaptive attack, using four standard benchmarks and three click models. RankGuard outperforms all baselines in most settings while being up to 62x more efficient than its closest competitors.

### [22] [Fair Comparison of Scheduling Algorithms on Heterogeneous Edge Clusters: A Continuous Adaptive Benchmark](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12343)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有CMMS算法比较困难，因为不同研究使用各自堆栈、单一工作负载且未报告每个决策的开销，缺乏公平统一的比较基准。

Result: 控制器排名高度依赖配置：轻负载下深度强化学习最优的控制器在负载加重时被规则启发式方法超越近29个百分点，且决策开销高约500倍；分离原始与稳态SLO能暴露切换成本。

Abstract: Modern Artificial Intelligence (AI) workloads deployed across the heterogeneous tiers of an edge--cloud continuum must satisfy multi-dimensional Service Level Objectives (SLOs) over latency, throughput, and output quality. For each incoming task, the scheduler picks both a target node and a processing mode (e.g., full or reduced inference precision). We call this class of problems \emph{Continuous Multi-Mode Scheduling} (CMMS). Comparing CMMS algorithms fairly is difficult because prior studies typically evaluate each controller in its own stack, under a single workload, and without reporting per-decision overhead. To close these gaps, we present an open source benchmark platform that features (i) a unified controller interface, (ii) a closed-loop workload driver covering multiple workload patterns, and (iii) dual-metric SLO scoring that reports raw SLO (overall compliance) and steady-state SLO (compliance during stable operation) separately. Running six controllers across five cluster configurations and two load regimes (424 episodes), we find that controller rankings are strongly configuration-dependent: a deep reinforcement-learning winner under light workloads loses to a rule-based heuristic by nearly 29 percentage points once load intensifies, at roughly 500$\times$ the per-decision operational overhead. We further show that separating raw from steady-state SLOs exposes switching costs that a single aggregate score would otherwise conflate.

### [23] [A PubMed-Scale Dataset of Structured Biomedical Abstracts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11361)

Method: 从完整PubMed数据库中提取2320万条记录，分为两个子集：590万条作者自结构化摘要（从官方XML解析），1720万条原始非结构化摘要（通过逐字提取的LLM流水线自动标注）。所有摘要统一为五部分格式，并保留原始PubMed标识符、发表类型和日期。

Abstract: Structured abstracts are important for biomedical literature processing, by facilitating information retrieval, text mining, and knowledge synthesis. To resolve this limitation, we introduce Structured PubMed, a comprehensive corpus of section-labeled biomedical abstracts compiled from the complete PubMed database, encompassing over 23.2 million research-article records. The corpus is divided into two distinct subsets: a collection of 5.9 million author-structured abstracts parsed from official XML files, and an automatically labeled collection of 17.2 million originally unstructured abstracts structured via a verbatim-extraction Large Language Model pipeline. Every record is harmonized under a unified five-section schema and mapped to its original PubMed identifier, publication type, and publication date. ### [24] [Factions Within, Uncertain Across: Within-Document Reader Sub-Groups in Social Highlighting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11613)
*Kazuki Nakayashiki,Keisuke Watanabe*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文研究读者群体在共同阅读同一文档时，其标注行为是否呈现内部派系结构，以及这种结构是否具有跨文档的稳定性。实验发现：同一文档内读者形成显著的子群体（派系），但该结构是否随读者跨文档迁移，因统计效力不足而无法确定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨群体标注行为的内在结构：多人高亮同一文档时，是形成统一共识，还是存在因读者子群体不同而标注内容差异的现象？以及这种结构是源于读者自身特质还是文档特征？

Method: 基于共读平台数据，采用保边界的curveball零模型进行两个实验：实验1分析文档内读者子群体结构；实验2通过跨文档分裂半复现检验和效力校准，评估读者配对的稳定性。

Result: 实验1：读者在文档内形成强子群体，配对一致性远超随机预期（最近邻一致性z=+6.3，88%文档显著），其中约40%可归因于共享文档区域关注，多数为更精细的读者特异性一致（z=+3.6，77%显著）。实验2：跨文档分裂半复现近乎零（+0.078和0.000），仅高重叠配对（k≥4）的点估计为正但不显著且不精确。

Conclusion: 文档内的群体标注呈现派系化结构，但该结构是否为稳定的读者特质跨文档迁移，由于数据限制无法得出结论，数据兼容从情境性分组到弱至中度稳定特质的各种解释。

Abstract: When many people highlight the same document, is the crowd a single consensus, or is it internally structured into reader sub-groups that mark different things -- and is that structure a stable property of a reader or of the document? Building on prior work showing an individual's within-document highlighting signal is a whisper while individuality lives in selection, we ask the group-level question on a co-readership platform using a margin-preserving curveball null. Experiment 1: within a document, readers form strong sub-groups -- pairs agree far beyond what shared salience, mark density, and sentence popularity predict (nearest-neighbour agreement z=+6.3, significant in 88% of documents). Under an eight-block region-preserving null, shared engagement with the same coarse regions of the document accounts for about 40% of this excess; the majority survives as finer reader-specific agreement (z=+3.6, 77% significant). So the within-document crowd is, in a descriptive sense, factional. Experiment 2: is that grouping a stable reader trait? Here we are honest about power. The cross-document split-half reproducibility of a pair's agreement is near zero pooled (+0.078 and 0.000 in two separately drawn samples), and a power calibration shows the test is informative only for pairs that co-read many documents. In the only informative high-overlap subset (k>=4), point estimates are positive but small-sample, imprecise across the separately drawn samples, never significant, and attenuate under the region-preserving null. We therefore leave cross-document stability unresolved: the data is consistent with anything from situational grouping to a weak-to-moderate stable reader trait. The crowd is factional within a document; whether its factions follow the reader across documents is, honestly, beyond our reach.

</details>


### [25] [The Long Tail, Not the Front Page: Cold-Start Prediction of Crowd Highlight Salience](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11654)
*Kazuki Nakayashiki,Keisuke Watanabe*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文研究能否在读者标注之前，通过文本预测文档中的群体关注点。作者训练了一个逻辑排序模型，结合句子嵌入和位置/上下文特征，在回顾性冷启动模拟中，比首句基线（lead baseline）平均精确率提升+0.044，精确率@3从0.25提升至0.39（+55%相对提升），且优势主要来自嵌入特征和训练增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 社交高亮工具最有用的信号是读者群体标记的段落，但这只有在对已被阅读的文档时才存在。作者想知道能否在文档积累读者标记之前，仅凭文本预测出群体的关注点（即文档的群体显著性）。

Method: 使用预注册的阶梯式模型（逻辑排序模型），基于句子嵌入和位置/上下文特征进行训练；采用按文档聚类的自助法（bootstrap）进行统计检验；与首句基线（lead baseline）及两种无监督抽取式基线（centroid、LexRank式中心性）进行对比；通过消融实验和标准化回归分析优势来源。

Result: 训练模型比首句基线平均精确率提升+0.044（95% CI [+0.029, +0.058]），在97%的重采样中超过预注册的边界delta=0.03；精确率@3从0.25提升至0.39（+55%相对提升），模型在69%的文档上优于首句基线。无监督基线均不如首句基线。优势主要来自原始嵌入（+0.014）和训练增强（+0.010）。

Conclusion: 通过训练可以从小样本读者标记中学习到文本显著性信号，在回顾性冷启动模拟中取得稳健但较小的优势。优势主要由文档流行度（越低优势越大）和标签可靠性决定，在最热门内容上优势几乎消失（原因是首句基线变强而非模型变弱）。

Abstract: A social highlighter's most useful signal -- which passages a crowd of readers marks -- exists only for documents people have already read. Can the aggregate crowd salience of a document be predicted from its text before its marks accumulate? Prior work on this data found that zero-shot language models recover highlight locations worse than a trivial lead (position) baseline, so we ask whether a model trained on the highlight corpus can beat that baseline. Using a pre-registered ladder of models and a by-document cluster bootstrap, we find a small but robust edge: a logistic ranker over sentence embeddings and positional/contextual features beats the lead baseline by +0.044 average precision (95% CI [+0.029, +0.058]; clears a pre-registered margin delta=0.03 in 97% of resamples, and stable across pipeline re-runs). Two unsupervised extractive baselines (centroid, LexRank-style centrality) lose to lead, and the trained model beats them by +0.108, so the edge is not recovered by generic unsupervised proxies -- it reflects learning from real reader marks. In product terms, precision@3 rises from 0.25 to 0.39 (+55% relative) and the model beats lead on 69% of documents. An ablation attributes the edge to the raw embedding (+0.014) and training augmentation (+0.010), each with a positive CI. The edge is not a temporal-generalization failure, and we find no evidence that content drift or near-duplicate leakage explains it. A standardized regression shows the advantage is governed mainly by document popularity (lower popularity, larger edge) and by label reliability. It nearly vanishes only on the most popular content; there it is the lead baseline that strengthens, not the model that weakens. Because our evaluation conditions on documents that eventually accumulated readers, these results are a retrospective cold-start simulation.

</details>


### [26] [CompRank: Efficient LLM Reranking via Token-Level Compression and Decoding-Free Scoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11700)
*Xuan Lu,Haohang Huang,Yingqi Fan,Junlong Tong,Yuxuan Zhang,Ping Nie,Rui Meng,Xiaoyu Shen*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 提出CompRank框架，通过令牌压缩和注意力评分机制，在仅保留10.2%文档令牌的情况下，实现与全令牌注意力相当的排序性能，并带来最高9.5倍的速度提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM重排序器计算成本高昂，难以应用于长候选列表，亟需一种令牌高效的重排序框架来降低计算开销。

Method: 将文档表示与候选顺序和查询上下文解耦，实现可重用的文档侧状态；采用分段令牌压缩减少查询-文档交互成本；引入CopyNet风格目标函数，直接对齐基于注意力的文档评分与训练监督。

Result: 在BEIR数据集上，仅保留10.2%文档令牌，NDCG@10达到39.2（全令牌为39.7）；在TREC-COVID上，对500文档候选列表排序稳定，端到端加速4.9-9.5倍。

Conclusion: 令牌级压缩与免解码注意力评分是实现可扩展LLM重排序的有效路径。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) rerankers have become an important component of modern retrieval and retrieval-augmented generation pipelines, but their high computational cost limits their applicability to long candidate lists. In this paper, we propose \textbf{CompRank}, a token-efficient reranking framework that reduces redundant computation by aligning reranker design with the sparsity of ranking signals. CompRank decouples document representations from candidate order and query context, enabling reusable document-side states; applies segment-wise token compression to reduce query--document interaction cost; and introduces a CopyNet-style objective that directly aligns attention-based document scoring with training supervision. Experiments on seven BEIR datasets show that CompRank achieves strong reranking performance while retaining only 10.2\% of document tokens, reaching an average NDCG@10 of 39.2 compared with 39.7 under full-token attention. Further scaling experiments on TREC-COVID show that CompRank remains stable when evaluated on candidate lists of up to 500 documents after training on 30-document lists, while achieving $4.9\times$--$9.5\times$ end-to-end speedup over generation-based listwise reranking and approximately $1.3\times$ speedup over the full-token CompRank variant. These results suggest that token-level compression and decoding-free attention scoring provide an effective path toward scalable LLM-based reranking.

</details>


### [27] [FAST-MEL: A Fast, Accurate, and Storage Efficient Solution for Multimodal Entity Linking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11749)
*Derrien Thomas,Laurent Amsaleg,Pascale Sébillot*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出FAST-MEL，一种轻量级多模态实体链接系统，通过紧凑的固定大小向量表示文本和视觉信息，在保持高精度的同时实现了三个数量级的加速和一个数量级的存储压缩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MEL系统无法同时满足高链接精度、计算效率和存储效率这三个实际部署的关键需求。

Method: 提出FAST-MEL，采用轻量级编码器架构，为每个实体和提及构建紧凑的固定大小向量化表示，同时编码文本和视觉信息。

Result: 匹配最佳系统的链接精度，但速度快三个数量级，存储消耗比最快系统低一个数量级。

Conclusion: FAST-MEL在精度、速度和存储三者之间取得了最优平衡，适用于大规模实际场景。

Abstract: Multimodal entity linking (MEL) is the task that consists of matching textual and visual mentions of entities in unstructured data to their corresponding entities in a knowledge base (KB). To be effective in large-scale practical settings, MEL systems must meet three objectives: high linking accuracy, computational efficiency, and storage efficiency, i.e., a compact yet efficient index of the KB. In this paper, we highlight that state-of-the-art systems fail to simultaneously satisfy these 3 requirements. To meet this three-fold objective, we propose FAST-MEL, a lightweight encoder-based MEL solution that relies on a novel and compact fixed-size vectorized representation of both the textual and visual information of each entity or mention. It matches the accuracy of the best systems but performs three orders of magnitude faster. It also consumes one order of magnitude less storage than the fastest systems.

### [28] [What Limits Does Quantization Place on Dense Top-$k$ Retrieval? A Theoretical Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11780)
*Koki Okajima,Tsukasa Yoshida*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文证明，在有限精度（量化）条件下，实现完美top-k检索所需的嵌入维度d必须随语料库大小N对数增长，且存在精度阈值B*，低于该阈值则无论维度多高都无法实现完美检索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前人工作表明在无限精度下，d=O(k)即可实现独立于N的完美top-k检索嵌入；本文旨在探究实际有限精度场景下这一结论是否仍然成立，揭示精度限制对嵌入维度的影响。

Method: 理论上证明完美top-k检索需要Bd=Ω(k ln N)；针对ℓ2归一化B比特均匀标量量化模型，推导出精度阈值B*=O(ln ln N)及不同精度-维度的可行区域边界。

Result: 1) 有限精度下维度必须随语料库大小对数增长；2) 存在精度阈值，低于该阈值无任何维度可达成完美检索；3) 刻画了可行(B, d)对的多个区域。

Conclusion: 在实际向量数据库和稠密检索系统中，量化是标配手段，因此嵌入维度和精度必须随语料库规模增长，这对现有系统的设计有重要指导意义。

Abstract: We establish conditions for embedding a corpus of $N$ documents as $d$-dimensional vectors such that every $k$-subset $S \subseteq [N]$ is realizable as a result of top-$k$ retrieval by some query vector. Recent work shows that $d = O(k)$ suffices for such embeddings to exist in $\mathbb{R}^d$, independently of $N$. We theoretically prove that this corpus-independent bound is specific to infinite precision. With $B$ bits per coordinate, perfect top-$k$ retrieval requires $Bd = Ω(k \ln N)$; thus, at any fixed precision, the dimension must grow at least logarithmically with $N$. Specializing to a $\ell_2$-normalized $B$-bit uniform scalar quantization model, we also identify a threshold on the precision $B^{*} = O(\ln \ln N)$ below which no dimension suffices, together with two further regimes that bound the feasible $(B, d)$ pairs. Our result implies that in practical vector databases and dense retrieval systems where quantization is standard, the embedding dimension and possibly the precision must grow with the corpus size.

</details>

To address this gap, we introduce CORE-Bench, a comprehensive benchmark for code retrieval in the era of agentic coding. ### [30] [Tail-Aware Adaptive-k: Query-Adaptive Context Selection for Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11907)
*Ziyu Song,Jiaming Fang,Kuangyu Li,Tuo Xia,Chuanpeng Wang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 提出TAA-k框架，利用极值理论和局部验证策略实现RAG系统中自适应上下文选择，在保持统计严谨性的同时大幅降低计算复杂度，达到接近oracle的检索质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG系统采用固定Top-K检索无法适应查询依赖和重尾相似度分布，而全局极值方法计算成本高且统计不稳定。

Method: 通过膝点检测识别候选区域，再在该窗口内应用EVT拟合优度检验验证尾部行为起始点，实现从粗到精的自适应截断。

Result: 在WebQuestions、2WikiMultiHopQA、MuSiQue上F1接近oracle（差距2-3%），计算复杂度从O(N²M)降至O(√(N log N)·M)。

Conclusion: TAA-k是一种训练免费、高效鲁棒的自适应检索截断方法，在不同嵌入模型和压缩维度下表现稳定。

Abstract: Adaptive context selection is critical for retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems, as fixed Top-K retrieval fails under query-dependent and heavy-tailed similarity distributions. While Extreme Value Theory (EVT) offers a principled framework for adaptive truncation, existing approaches apply EVT globally across the entire ranked list, incurring prohibitive computational costs and statistical instability. We propose Tail-Aware Adaptive-k(TAA-k), a training-free framework that operationalizes EVT through a localized validation strategy. The key insight is that ranked similarity curves exhibit a characteristic steep--flat--steep pattern reflecting a transition from relevance-dominated to noise-dominated regimes. TAA-k exploits this geometric structure via knee detection to identify a compact candidate region, then applies EVT-based goodness-of-fit testing within this window to validate the onset of tail behavior. This coarse-to-fine design reduces computational complexity from O(N^2M) to O(sqrt{N\log N}*M) while maintaining statistical rigor. Under mild monotone likelihood ratio assumptions, TAA-k yields a stable, query-adaptive cutoff corresponding to the earliest noise-dominated position. Experiments on WebQuestions, 2WikiMultiHopQA, and MuSiQue demonstrate that TAA-k achieves near-oracle retrieval quality (F1 within 2-3% of oracle) with orders-of-magnitude efficiency gains over global EVT methods, while maintaining robustness across embedding models and compression dimensions.

Our method generates natural-language user interest personas that address the exploitation-exploration trade-off by combining the summarization of existing interests with novel topics, directly during serving. To overcome the computational challenges of online LLM inference at a billion-user scale, we design a cost-efficient architecture leveraging knowledge distillation, asynchronous inference, and input optimization via semantically clustered video representations. Extensive offline evaluations, user studies, and live A/B tests demonstrate significant improvements in viewer value. ### [32] [DiffCold: A Diffusion-based Generative Model for Cold-Start Item Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12245)
*Kangning Zhang,Yingjie Qin,Weinan Zhang,Yong Yu,Jianghao Lin*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: DiffCold是一种基于扩散生成模型的方法，通过条件扩散从内容特征重建物品嵌入，解决了冷启动物品推荐的“跷跷板困境”（冷热物品性能此消彼长的问题），在三个基准数据集上全面超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有冷启动物品推荐方法普遍存在“跷跷板困境”：提升冷物品性能会损害热物品性能，反之亦然。作者识别出根本原因是冷热物品嵌入存在分布差异（行为流形 vs 语义流形），而现有方法强行映射导致表征精度损失。

Method: 提出DiffCold框架，核心是条件扩散模型从内容特征重建热物品嵌入，保留流形结构。包含两个关键设计：1）检索增强聚合器（利用语义相似热物品初始化生成，减少噪声）；2）基于模拟的表征对齐模块（通过对比学习确保生成嵌入与真实嵌入分布一致）。

Result: 在三个基准数据集上，DiffCold在所有评估指标上一致优于现有最先进方法，有效解决了跷跷板困境。

Conclusion: DiffCold通过扩散生成模型统一冷热物品表征，在不牺牲热物品性能的前提下提升冷物品推荐效果，为冷启动推荐提供了新范式。

Abstract: Cold-start item recommendation remains a persistent challenge in real-world systems due to the absence of interaction histories. While prior models attempt to bridge this gap using item content features, they universally suffer from the \textbf{seesaw dilemma}: enhancing performance for cold items inevitably degrades performance for warm items, and vice versa. We identify that this dilemma stems from a fundamental \textbf{distributional disparity}: warm item embeddings occupy a complex ``behavioral manifold" shaped by rich interaction signals, whereas cold item embeddings are constrained to a ``semantic manifold" derived solely from auxiliary content. Existing methods often force a rigid mapping between these inconsistent spaces, causing the model to sacrifice the precision of warm representations to accommodate cold ones. To address this, we propose \textbf{DiffCold}, a diffusion-based generative model that unifies warm and cold representations. Unlike GANs or VAEs, DiffCold leverages conditional diffusion to reconstruct warm item embeddings from content, preserving the underlying manifold structure without degradation. We further tailor this paradigm with two specific designs: a \textbf{Retrieval-enhanced Aggregator} that initializes generation using semantically similar warm items to bypass inefficient noise, and a \textbf{Simulation-based Representation Alignment} module that enforces distribution consistency between generated and real embeddings via contrastive learning. Experiments on three benchmarks confirm that DiffCold resolves the seesaw dilemma, consistently outperforming state-of-the-art methods across all metrics.

</details>

This tutorial synthesizes the algorithms, systems, and design principles driving these converging directions, offering data science and data mining researchers a unified perspective on integrating LLMs, graph data management, graph mining, graph ML, and agentic computation into next-generation graph-native AI systems.

### [34] [Querying Cohesive Subgraph regarding Span-Constrained Triangles on Temporal Graphs with Dynamic Index Maintenance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11582)
*Chuhan Hu,Ming Zhong,Lei Li*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种面向时序图的(k,δ)-truss结构，要求三角形在短时间窗口内存在，兼具静态和时序凝聚性。作者设计了无索引和基于索引的查询方法，利用双包含关系将索引压缩为图或树结构，显著降低存储开销并支持最优时间检索。实验表明，基于索引的方法比无索引方法快2~4个数量级，压缩比可达10^{-4}，且支持高效动态更新。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时序图研究的发展使得传统静态图概念（如三角形、k-核）被重新定义。现有k-truss缺乏对时序信息的考虑，无法捕捉时序图中的时间凝聚性。因此，本文引入(k,δ)-truss，要求三角形在足够短的时间窗口内存在，以同时保证图的结构稳定性和时间连贯性。

Method: 定义(k,δ)-truss结构；提出无索引和基于索引两种查询方法；利用双包含关系设计基于图和树的索引结构，实现无损压缩；提出基于truss分解和truss维护的两种索引构建算法，减少冗余计算；设计索引的动态维护技术。

Conclusion: (k,δ)-truss是传统k-truss在时序图上的有效扩展，所提索引方法在查询效率、存储压缩和动态维护方面均表现出显著优势，适用于大规模时序图分析。

Abstract: Recent advances in temporal graph research have redefined traditional static graph concepts such as triangles, motifs, and $k$-cores. Inspired by this, we introduce a novel $(k,δ)$-truss for temporal graphs, requiring triangles to exist within sufficiently short time windows. The $(k,δ)$-truss ensures both static and temporal cohesion, while the original $k$-truss is a special case when $δ= \infty$. To address $(k,δ)$-truss queries, we propose index-free and index-based approaches. Utilizing the dual containment relation of $(k,δ)$-trusses, our indexes losslessly compress all $(k,δ)$-trusses into map or tree structures, significantly reducing space while enabling optimal-time retrieval. To scale to large temporal graphs, we develop two index construction algorithms based on truss decomposition and truss maintenance, respectively, which substantially reduce redundant computations. Moreover, we present techniques for the dynamic maintenance of the proposed indexes. The experimental results demonstrate that index-based approaches process queries in interactive time and outperform the index-free approach by 2$\sim$4 orders of magnitude, while the indexes achieve compression ratios of up to $10^{-4}$ and can be updated efficiently without rebuilding from scratch.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度学习方法要么将数据库转为图结构（如GNN），要么通过嵌入+查询扩展的方式处理关系数据。作者希望提出一个统一的形式化框架，将关系推理与可学习的神经组件自然融合，实现一种既能被视为带可训练组件的查询计划、又能被视为内嵌关系结构的神经架构的通用方法。

Method: NRPs扩展了Datalog风格规则，引入对向量嵌入的结合、聚合和变换操作。通过定义不同语法片段（零元、一元、前沿守卫NRPs）来恢复现有架构（如GNN消息传递、Deep Homomorphism Networks），并使用FOCQ（一阶逻辑+计数）在实权重结构上的解释来刻画表达能力，建立与统一TC⁰电路复杂度在有序数据库上的精确联系。

Result: 零元NRPs对应非自适应查询算法；一元NRPs泛化GNN消息传递并精确捕获Deep Homomorphism Networks；前沿守卫NRPs适用于带行ID的数据库。无限制NRPs（使用ReLU-FFN变换）的表达能力由FOCQ刻画，并与有序数据库上的统一TC⁰复杂度精确对应。

Conclusion: NRPs是一个广泛的声明式框架，能够统一关系数据上的查询与神经计算，为理解现有神经架构间的关系以及设计新的可解释神经符号系统提供了理论基础。

Abstract: The conventional approach to deep learning over relational databases applies neural models, such as Graph Neural Networks (GNNs), to a graph representation of the database. Recent approaches instead operate on databases directly, associating tuples with embeddings and extending query mechanisms to jointly process embeddings and relational content. Inspired by these developments, we introduce Neuro-Relational Programs (NRPs), a declarative query language for relational databases whose facts carry numeric vector embeddings. NRPs extend Datalog-style rules with operations that combine, aggregate, and transform embeddings, thereby interleaving relational reasoning and learnable neural components within a single formalism. This yields a general approach to neural computation over relational data: an NRP can be read both as a query plan with trainable components and as a neural architecture with relational structure built in.
  Natural syntactic fragments of NRPs recover existing architectures and query formalisms. Zero-ary NRPs correspond to non-adaptive query algorithms; monadic NRPs generalize GNN-style message passing and precisely capture Deep Homomorphism Networks, a connection that we extend to frontier-guarded NRPs over databases with row-ids. We characterize the expressive power of unrestricted NRPs with ReLU-FFN transformations by FOCQ, an extension of first-order logic with counting interpreted over real-weighted structures, yielding a precise connection with uniform TC$^0$ over ordered databases. Together, these results establish NRPs as a broad declarative framework for querying and neural computation over relational data.

</details>


### [37] [TAHOE: Text-to-SQL with Automated Hint Optimization from Experience](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12387)
*Zhiyi Chen,Jie Song,Peng Li*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: Tahoe是一个通过动态提示优化来提升LLM Text-to-SQL能力的系统，它将调试跟踪转化为结构化的提示库，在不更新模型参数的情况下显著提升了SQL生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM驱动的Text-to-SQL从原型到生产面临诸多困难：真实部署需要处理严格的SQL方言、庞大的数据库模式以及不断演变的用户偏好，而监督微调成本高昂且僵化，基于智能体的测试时扩展同样代价不菲。因此需要一种更高效、动态的提示优化方法。

Method: Tahoe提出将提示优化视为动态数据管理问题。核心包括：(1) 错误驱动的提示学习流水线，将调试跟踪整合为结构化提示库；(2) 语法提示（Syntax Hints）用于方言规则，语义提示（Semantic Hints）用于模式和用户特定逻辑；(3) 策略层（Strategy Layer）建模冲突的用户意图，包含成功、危害、惰性和支持等经验统计信号；(4) 推理时通过逻辑规划（Logic Planning）和SQL合成（SQL Synthesis）引导LLM。

Result: 在Spider 2.0-Snow基准上，使用GPT-5.5时通过率从61.95%提升至79.42%，pass-at-4从72.57%提升至87.61%，Snowflake语法通过率达100%，编译器反馈轮次从2.79降至0.12。提示库还可迁移至弱骨干模型（Doubao-2.0-lite提升19.7个百分点）。

Conclusion: Tahoe通过结构化的提示优化方法，在不更新模型参数的情况下显著提升了Text-to-SQL的性能，证明了将提示优化视为数据管理问题的有效性。部署阶段的人机反馈更新留作未来工作。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have democratized database access through Text-to-SQL, but moving from prototypes to production remains difficult. Real deployments must handle strict SQL dialects, massive schemas, and evolving user preferences, while supervised fine-tuning is costly and rigid and agentic test-time scaling is expensive. We present Tahoe, a system that treats prompt optimization as a dynamic data management problem. Tahoe uses an error-driven hint learning pipeline across Development and Deployment to consolidate debugging traces into a structured Hint Bank. Compiler feedback is distilled into reusable Syntax Hints for dialect-specific rules, while execution and user feedback are converted into Semantic Hints for schema- and user-specific logic. Tahoe further introduces a Strategy Layer that models conflicting user intents as competing strategies under shared natural-language triggers, with recency signals and post-learning attribution statistics that summarize empirical success, harm, inertness, and support. At inference time, Tahoe retrieves relevant hints and guides the LLM through Logic Planning followed by SQL Synthesis. We implement and evaluate the development-phase workflow, leaving deployment-time human-feedback updates for future work. On Spider 2.0-Snow, Tahoe substantially improves Text-to-SQL without updating model parameters. On 113 supervised Spider 2.0-Snow-0212 examples using GPT-5.5, Tahoe raises pass rate from 61.95 percent to 79.42 percent and pass-at-4 from 72.57 percent to 87.61 percent, achieves 100 percent Snowflake syntax pass rate, and reduces average compiler-feedback critic rounds from 2.79 to 0.12 per sampled candidate. The same Hint Bank also transfers to weaker backbones, including a 19.7 percentage-point pass-rate gain on Doubao-2.0-lite.

</details>

### [38] [Restless bandits with imperfect binary feedback: PCL-indexability analysis and computation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11192)
*José Niño-Mora*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对具有二元潜在状态和不完美二元反馈的 restless bandits 问题，提出了基于部分守恒律（PCL）的分析与计算框架，用于建立可索引性并计算 Whittle 指数，实验表明该策略显著优于基准策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受机会频谱接入中传感误差问题的驱动，研究具有二元潜在状态和不完美二元反馈的 restless bandits 的可索引性与 Whittle 指数求解。

Method: 基于 PCL 框架，结合确定性骨架、更新分解和组合词论分析随机动力学；在阈值区域导出折扣奖励和资源度量的闭式表达式以验证 PCL 可索引性条件；在无法完全解析验证的区域，设计数值方案计算边际度量与边际生产率（MP）指数。

Result: 在多数参数范围内验证了可索引性条件，MP 指数策略在计算实验中显著优于标准基准策略。

Conclusion: 所提出的 PCL 框架有效解决了该复杂 restless bandits 问题的可索引性分析与 Whittle 指数计算，MP 指数策略具有优越的性能表现。

Abstract: We study restless bandits with binary latent states and imperfect binary feedback, motivated by opportunistic spectrum access with sensing errors. For the associated belief-state model, we develop a partial conservation laws (PCL)-based analytical and computational framework for establishing indexability and evaluating the Whittle index, building on a verification theorem for real-state discounted restless bandits. The framework analyzes the stochastic dynamics via an associated deterministic skeleton, renewal decompositions, and combinatorics on words. It yields tractable expressions for discounted reward and resource metrics in several threshold regimes, enabling full verification of the PCL-indexability conditions there. For the remaining regime, where a complete analytic verification is not achieved in this paper, we derive efficient numerical schemes for computing the relevant marginal metrics and the marginal productivity (MP) index, which equals the Whittle index when those conditions hold. Extensive computational experiments provide strong evidence that these conditions also hold in that regime across broad parameter ranges and without the stringent parameter restrictions imposed in prior work. The experiments further show that theMP index policy typically outperforms standard benchmark policies, often by a substantial margin.

### [39] [To Intervene or Not: Guiding Inference-time Alignment with Probabilistic Model Blending](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11201)
*Jin Gan,Xin Li,Jun Luo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: BlendIn是一个推理时对齐框架，通过质量感知对齐和按可靠性比例加权混合模型知识，解决现有对齐方法中指导信号不可靠导致过度干预的问题，最高可提升50%性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推理时对齐方法从对齐模型中提取指导信号，但未评估其可靠性；系统评估发现指导有效性在不同模型间差异巨大，无效指导会导致进一步混乱和过度干预，性能较差。

Method: 提出BlendIn框架：从二元决策转为创建混合分布，整合两个模型的知识；进行质量感知对齐，根据可靠性按比例加权每个模型的贡献；保留有益的指导信号，降低不可靠建议的权重。

Result: 在具有挑战性的模型对上实现了持续且最高达50%的性能提升；提供了对齐不良指导的诊断信号和缓解策略。

Conclusion: BlendIn通过质量感知和比例加权的方式稳定了推理时对齐，有效解决了指导信号不可靠导致的过度干预问题，显著提升了模型对齐的性能。

Abstract: The wide deployment of LLMs has made model alignment necessary to make newly trained models safely and effectively respond to user instructions. Among different methods, inference-time alignment is often cheaper as it intervenes (i.e., offers guidances) only during output generation. Existing proposals apply guidances extracted from certain aligned models without properly assessing their reliability. Nonetheless, our systematic evaluation reveals that guidance effectiveness varies drastically across models; since ineffective guidances lead to further confusion and thus further interventions, the resulting excessive interventions typically indicate poor performance. To make interventions more effective and thus more efficient, we introduce BlendIn, an inference-time alignment framework that shifts from binary decisions to creating hybrid distributions integrating both models' knowledge. BlendIn stabilizes inference-time alignment by performing quality-aware alignment and proportionally weighting each model's contribution based on reliability. Compared with existing works, it preserves beneficial guidance while downweighting unreliable suggestions. BlendIn provides both diagnostic signals and mitigation strategies for misaligned guidance, achieving consistent and up to 50% performance improvement on challenging model pairs. Our code is available at: https://github.com/DecayingSeart/BlendIn.

</details>


### [40] [Dual-Stance Evaluation of Sycophancy: The Structure of Agreement and the Limits of Intervention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11205)
*Matthew James Buchan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文发现，虽然模型在几何空间中区分了谄媚和事实性同意，但通过质心差引导法进行激活操纵时，这两种行为无法被差异化调控，导致减少谄媚的同时也抑制了正确事实的同意（如“地球是圆的”），揭示了表示可读与可写之间的普遍鸿沟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有激活引导技术（如减少谄媚）的评估通常只测试单一方位，未检验是否误伤了对事实正确陈述的同意，作者因此引入双立场评估方法来填补这一评估空白。

Method: 提出双立场评估（dual-stance evaluation），对每个话题同时测试两个立场；采用质心差引导法（centroid-difference steering）对Llama-3-8B-Instruct进行干预，分析谄媚与事实性同意在激活空间中的几何关系。

Result: 模型在几何上确实将谄媚和事实性同意的表示分离到不同子空间，但引导方向在两者上的投影几乎相同，无法差异性地仅减少谄媚；实际干预中同时降低了谄媚和正确事实的同意比例。

Conclusion: 揭示了“表示可读但不可写”的普遍问题：即使能从激活中读出两种行为的区别，也无法通过简单的残差流操纵来差异化干预，这可能是生成动态或更精细结构导致的。

Abstract: Activation steering can shift LLM behaviour, but standard evaluations do not typically test whether a sycophancy-reduction direction also suppresses agreement with factually correct statements. We introduce dual-stance evaluation, which tests both stances of each topic, and apply it to centroid-difference steering on Llama-3-8B-Instruct. We find a dissociation: the model represents sycophantic and factual agreement in geometrically distinct subspaces, yet the steering direction projects equally onto both and cannot differentially target either. The direction accordingly reduces agreement with factually correct statements (e.g. that the Earth is round) as well as sycophantic ones. All other static properties of the two activation groups are matched, suggesting the behavioural dissociation arises from generation dynamics or from finer-grained structure that residual-stream analysis cannot resolve. The pattern illustrates a general gap: representations that are readable from activations may not be writable through them.

</details>


### [41] [Few-Shot Resampling for Scalable Statistically-Sound Data Mining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11235)
*Leonardo Pellegrina,Fabio Vandin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出FewRS方法，通过仅需生成和分析极少量的重采样数据集，就能在数据挖掘结果统计显著性评估中提供严格的假阳性控制，相比现有方法将运行时间降低两个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有重采样方法需要生成和分析数千个重采样数据集，在处理大规模数据或计算密集型分析时效率低下，难以实际应用。

Method: FewRS基于推导出的检验统计量极值偏差的新上界，仅需极少量重采样数据集即可评估统计显著性，并具有严格的假阳性发现概率保证。

Result: 在模式挖掘和网络分析等任务上，相比现有方法运行时间降低最多两个数量级，同时保持高统计功效。

Conclusion: FewRS是一种简单、有效且高度可扩展的重采样方法，适用于各类数据挖掘结果的统计显著性评估，能够在大型真实数据集上实现统计验证。

Abstract: A key step in knowledge discovery is the evaluation of data mining results. In several applications, including pattern mining, graph analysis, and others, this step includes the evaluation of the statistical significance of the results, to avoid spurious discoveries due only to noise or random fluctuations in the data. While specialized procedures have been developed for some specific applications, resampling-based approaches are widely used, in particular for complex analyses where analytical results cannot be derived. However, current resampling-based approaches require the generation and analysis of thousands of resampled datasets, and are therefore impractical for large datasets or computationally intensive analyses.
  In this paper, we introduce FewRS, a simple and effective resampling-based approach to assess the statistical significance of data mining results with rigorous guarantees on the probability of false discoveries. Our approach can be used in every situation where resampling-based approaches are applied. FewRS builds on our derivation of a novel bound to the supremum deviation of test statistics representing the quality of data mining results. We prove that FewRS needs to generate and analyze an extremely small number of resampled datasets, leading to a highly scalable approach with wide applicability. We test our approach on common tasks such as pattern mining and network analysis. In all cases, our approach results in a reduction of up to two orders of magnitude in running time compared to the state of the art, while preserving high statistical power, enabling the statistical validation of data mining results on large-scale real-world datasets.

</details>


### [42] [ProHiFlo: Hierarchical Flow Matching with Functional Guidance for De Novo Protein Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11243)
*Chuanzhen Wang,Meade Cleti,Pete Jano*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ProHiFlo是一个分层流匹配框架，通过粗到细生成、功能引导和自适应SE(3)等变架构，在蛋白质从头生成任务上达到SOTA性能，采样步骤减少4倍，酶活性位点支架成功率58.9%优于RFDiffusion的41.2%。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有扩散和流匹配方法通常在单一分辨率下操作，且缺乏融入功能约束的机制，难以满足蛋白质设计中对特定功能特性的需求。

Method: 提出ProHiFlo框架，包含三个创新：(1)粗到细生成——先建模主链几何再细化到全原子坐标；(2)功能引导——利用预训练预测器引导生成朝向所需性质；(3)自适应SE(3)等变架构——实现高效多尺度处理。

Result: 在无条件生成、基序支架和功能设计任务上达到SOTA性能，采样步骤减少4倍；酶活性位点支架成功率达58.9%，显著优于RFDiffusion的41.2%。

Abstract: De novo protein generation has transformative potential in therapeutic design, enzyme engineering, and synthetic biology. While diffusion-based and flow matching approaches have achieved progress, they typically operate at single resolution and lack mechanisms for incorporating functional constraints. We introduce ProHiFlo, a hierarchical flow matching framework with three innovations: (1) coarse-to-fine generation that models backbone geometry before refining to all-atom coordinates, reducing computational cost while maintaining accuracy; (2) functional guidance leveraging pretrained predictors to steer generation toward desired properties without retraining; (3) adaptive SE(3)-equivariant architecture for efficient multi-scale processing. Experiments on unconditional generation, motif scaffolding, and functional design demonstrate state-ofthe-art performance while requiring 4 fewer sampling steps. On enzyme active site scaffolding, ProHiFlo achieves 58.9% success rate compared to 41.2% for RFDiffusion.

*Yaser Mike Banad,Sarah Sharif*
